Recognized Organizations and Accredited Representatives Roster by State and City

Report Last Updated on: 04/21/25

Disclaimer: The DOJ R&A Program maintains rosters of Recognized Organizations and Accredited Representatives and makes these rosters available to the public. The contact information posted in these rosters is provided to the R&A Program by the Recognized Organizations. Each Recognized Organization has a duty to notify the R&A Program, through formal correspondence, of any changes to its contact information, such as name, address, and telephone number. While the R&A Program posts the most current information it receives, each Recognized Organization is responsible for promptly providing the R&A Program with the most recent changes in order for the information posted on the rosters to remain up to date.

• Search by Alphabetical Order or press [Ctrl] + [F] to find a representative. • Asterisk * denotes pending renewal.
